< Text>
My boyfriend and I showed up on a Saturday morning-ish, around 11:30. We were told that it was a 30 minute wait. After some time (didnâ€™t keep track but we were very hungry) we were offered to sit at the bar, we declined and were set on table seating. The restaurant itself is cute, nicely decorated and has a Wes Anderson movie playing on a tv behind the bar.
After getting seated and being served a glass of water (we had gotten coffee while waiting for our table) we were then informed that they were out of the breakfast potatoes and the eggs Benedict (and a couple other items) this was around 12-12:30.
The entire reason for visiting this particular place is because the eggs Benedict were so highly praised, so to say the least we were disappointed.
Instead I ordered the Wilshire omelette with hash browns (other option would have been breakfast potatoes) my boyfriend ordered the quiche of the day which happened to be the Wilshire quiche.
Our orders arrived quickly but the eggs in my omelette were significantly over cooked and the quiche was very spinach heavy and the dough was undercooked.
Our main disappointment stems from the fact that the two main dishes we wanted were sold out before we were seated. Had we known this we would have eaten somewhere else and avoided waiting 30 minutes and eating over cooked eggs.</Text>

<rate>4<//rate>< text>
Rialto Cafe is a popular Breakfast / Brunch Cafe in Downtown Fullerton. It's capacity is about 40-50, so yes it's small, and yes it's popular, so yes you will have to wait. You can't rush people to finish their food, pay and leave. On the other hand, when you do sit down and are paying for a service, you should be served in a appropriate way. The food should come out in timely manner, and yes you shouldn't wait to get your check cuz that won't help the ladder. That's what I experienced at Rialto today, the food is delicious, got the Smaoked dsalmon scrambler and eggs Benedict, both good. I would have them again, but yes I agree with the negative feedback about the service. It's a bit slow, the food takes a long time to come out and they maybe under staffed.

If you don't mind the wait but do want to enjoy some good food them give them a try.<//text>

<Text>June 18,: I wish we had the names of these serious servers because they were really great ) We met our friend from Atlanta before the rodeo at the Rialto adjacent to the Marriott where he was staying. It was happy hour and really busy but we managed to get 3 seats at the bar next to the service bar. The young woman who was bartending acknowledged me immediately and took our order immediately. Happy hour menu was super reasonable and thatâ€™s what we had for dinner. A couple of orders of steak tacos, some ribs, some calamari. All well prepared and tasty. The ribs were dry rubbed which I like much better than having sauce drip all over. When she was getting crazy busy another young lady bartender came over and offered our refills without us having to ask. We returned after the rodeo for a nightcap, the cocktail waitress was really nice, brought water without being asked ( she must have read my mind) and was prompt with drinks, refills and had such a fun personality. Although it was closing time and she was cleaning up and doing her side work at the tables she never rushed us to leave. We live north of Denver and of course, I used TripAdvisor to research where we were going to eat. Once I realized we were going to be short of time I noted that the Rialto was adjacent to the Marriott which would save us time and was convenient to the busses. The prices were extremely reasonable for downtown Denver and the food was darn good. If you are in Denver I highly recommend this place, we like to sit at the bar, there are many high top tables surrounding the bar which we sat at when we came back the second time and the bar was full. The dining room looked comfortable. The only thing that bothered me was the level of the music, it was really loud and made conversation slightly difficult for more than two so if I could tell the management to turn it down a couple of notches I would.<//Text>< UserId.>

<Text>(Current COVID-19 review)

So far I've been here quite a few times already. The drinks here are pretty consistent and they offer delivery and online ordering.  My constant go to drink is their Sunright Boba Milk Tea, the balance Of sweet and tea is excellent and when my gf came with me to try a fruit tea she said it was really good and their strawberry tea can rival Omomo. Lines here are usually short and workers here try to push drinks out fast, I do recommend 75% sugar since their milk tea drink can lean to be very sweet so 75% is good also ice level there is no need to adjust they don't put too much ice. I recommend this place, they do offer seating but it's closed currently due to COVID-19, and it's inside the OC mix next to Portolo Coffee. Happy boba drinking. They don't offer physical stamp cards but you can sign up for a rewards points on their iPad on the register and it'll link your card to your account, to later earn points for drinks!< /Text><user_name>Yolanda Christensen</user_name>< rating>

<text>Quick stop with Quick service.<//text><Resp>{'time': 1615778273994, 'text': "Glad to know you enjoyed stopping by, Tim! We hope you're able to come back again soon. -OB"}<//Resp><Gmap_id>0x80ec139a08084543:0x10c57da42d2c4e6b<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
< Review>
Their overall menu is just what anyone can expect of a burger joint. Yet, unlike most other restaurants, they seem terrified of seasonings. There's no distinctive flavors! ðŸ˜–

For example, all of their fried food (fried zucchini, fried mushrooms, french fries, fried onion rings, etc) tastes only of one thing -- fry oil ðŸ¤¢. Their beef burger patties lack flavor, except for just the faint hints of salt and pepper. But even then, their burgers taste just like any unseasoned beef would.

Surprisingly though, I think the gyro is their best item on the menu (super strange for a burger restaurant that also has "Burger" in its name). Their gyro meat is fairly well seasoned with traditional Greek seasonings. I've wondered about this question for a long time though: why is it only topped with lettuce and white onion, and not with the traditional gyro toppings of lettuce, diced tomatoes, and *red* onion? (White onion? Really?) It's disgusting with it. The flavor profile of white onions completely clash with the flavor profiles in the gyro. This is because white onions have the strongest flavor out of all the other onion varieties; which is why they're perfect in Mexican food. Red onions on the other hand, are the best to use on gyros, because they are milder and slightly sweeter in flavor, which provides a really nice balance to the overall flavor of the gyro.

It just seems to me that the restaurant badly needs someone who is more qualified to oversee all of the food related decisions, than that of the current person performing this function. It would also be a huge bonus if this knew someone new enough about the flavor profiles of foods, because that knowledge can be used to promote and improve the restaurant's overall food quality.<//Review>

< review>
I hate to give a poor review however the owner did not care to talk to my wife and I. We asked to speak with him  and the cashier said that he was busy cooking. We said that was okay and we would wait until he had a minute. We saw him walk out the door 45 minutes later!

The reason we wanted to speak with him was because he did not have any wheelchair seating and we thought that we should point out that it was needed. When we placed our order we asked if they had a table that we could sit at with a wheelchair and the cashier said just pull it up to one of the booths and it will work. I started to explain that it would not work very well but she did not seem to care. When she brought out the food I asked to speak with the owner or manger and then she volunteered a table in the corner under the TV. It was full of booster seats and news papers. She said that she would clear if off for us if we wanted. At that point we were already making the booth work so we told her to just have the owner see us when he got caught up.

My wife and I do not want to sit over in a corner under a TV. Also before her injury we would often go to Orcutt Burger with a group, now due to the seating we are forced to go somewhere that has wheelchair seating.

The cost to fix a few of the tables so that you could pull a wheelchair up would be very little. Likely less then $500!

I am not sure however I think that they are in violation of some ADA laws! We would like to shop local however if we cannot get access then we are forced to go elsewhere.<//review>

< Review>
would like to start off by saying the food is great. If I could give 5 stars for food only, I would. The 1 star review is based off of service only. I haven't even ate my meal yet as I am flabbergasted by the type of service I received this evening and generally lost my appetite.
I've lived in orcutt for 15 years. I've been going to Orcutt burger since I can remember.. The food is amazing, but my god, their staff is completely inept. They get the order wrong 9 times out of 10 and do not care about their mistakes.. I always let it slide because it's usually taken care of by upper management.
Seriously, it is probably best to eat inside as that way you can check to see if your meal is correct right away. But I always check the bag when going through the drive-thru.
I checked the bag as I always do, and noticed that my fries did not have any seasoning, that I specifically asked for.. The short haired blonde girl "did not have a name tag and I only have server #18 'Heaven' on my receipt" took the order to fix their mistake and then handed it back to me within ten seconds.. I was curious that it took a short time to rectify the order, but I THOUGHT it was taken care of. So I pulled to the parking lot to double check, and low and behold. All they did was dump seasoning into the top of my bag and call it a day..
They literally just did enough on top to get me out of the drive thru. I was tempted to go back and ask what in the world was going on with their service, but obviously I will not be getting help from any of their staff on hand this evening.
It's not the lack of seasoning I'm upset about. I'm upset about the complete disregard to fix their own mistake.
I only made this account to post this. I was completely floored by the lack of consideration coming from the server this evening.</Review>
